07/07/23, 08:04 - Garima: The control word of the Intel 8259 Programmable Interrupt Controller (PIC) is an 8-bit value used to configure the behavior of the PIC. It is sent to the PIC on its data bus to set various parameters and modes of operation.

The control word consists of three main fields: the operation command, the interrupt mask, and the ICW (Initialization Command Word) mode. Here is the breakdown of the control word format:

Operation Command (OCW) Field (bits 7-5):

OCW3 (bits 7-5): These bits specify the specific operation command to be executed by the PIC.
Interrupt Mask (IMR) Field (bits 4-0):

These bits indicate the mask status of each interrupt line, where each bit corresponds to an interrupt request (IRQ) line. A set bit (1) in the mask disables the corresponding interrupt line, while a cleared bit (0) enables it.
Initialization Command Word (ICW) Mode:

The ICW mode specifies the initialization mode command. The ICW mode is sent as a separate command when initializing the PIC, and it is not included in the OCW field of the control word.
Please note that the specific

09/07/23, 19:45 - Gunjan Sharma: Procedural SQL: Procedural SQL refers to SQL statements that are executed in a procedural manner, where you explicitly specify the sequence of operations to be performed. It involves writing code that describes the step-by-step procedure to achieve a specific result. Procedural SQL is often used in programming languages that incorporate SQL, such as PL/SQL (used in Oracle databases) and T-SQL (used in Microsoft SQL Server). These languages allow the inclusion of procedural constructs like loops, conditions, and variables in SQL statements, enabling more complex and customized database operations.

Non-procedural SQL: Non-procedural SQL, also known as declarative SQL, focuses on describing what data is required rather than how to retrieve it. In non-procedural SQL, you specify the desired result without specifying the exact steps to achieve it. The database management system is responsible for figuring out the most efficient way to execute the query. The most common example of non-procedural SQL is the SELECT statement, where you specify the columns and conditions to retrieve the required data, but you don't explicitly state how the database should perform the retrieval.

14/07/23, 17:16 - Garima: In TCP (Transmission Control Protocol), the connection termination process is designed to be symmetric, meaning both the client and the server participate in terminating the connection. This ensures that both ends of the connection have an opportunity to clean up any resources and close the connection gracefully.

On the other hand, during the connection establishment process, the steps are asymmetric. The client initiates the connection by sending a SYN (synchronize) packet to the server, and the server responds with a SYN-ACK (synchronize-acknowledgment) packet. Finally, the client acknowledges the server's response with an ACK packet. This three-way handshake establishes the connection.

The reason for this asymmetry is related to security and the prevention of resource exhaustion attacks. By requiring the client to initiate the connection, it prevents malicious entities from flooding a server with connection requests. The server can choose to ignore or reject connection requests based on its resources and policies.

In the termination process, both the client and the server need to actively participate to ensure a clean closure of the connection. This involves exchanging FIN (finish) packets. When one end of the connection wants to terminate, it sends a FIN packet to indicate that it has no more data to send. The receiving end acknowledges the FIN packet and may continue to send any remaining data before sending its own FIN packet. This back-and-forth ensures that both sides have finished transmitting data before the connection is fully closed. Once both ends have exchanged FIN packets and received acknowledgments, the connection is considered terminated.

In summary, the symmetry in connection termination allows both the client and the server to clean up resources and ensure a proper closure of the connection, while the asymmetry in connection establishment helps protect servers from resource exhaustion attacks by requiring the client to initiate the connection.

31/07/23, 22:17 - Gunjan Sharma: class Solution {
  public:
    // Function to return Breadth First Traversal of given graph.
    vector<int> bfsOfGraph(int V, vector<int> adj[]) {
        vector<int> ans;

        queue<int> q;
        q.push(0);
        
        vector<int> vis(V, 0);
        vis[0] = 1;
        
        while(!q.empty()){
            int node = q.front();
            q.pop();
            
            ans.push_back(node);
            
            for(auto child : adj[node]){
                if(!vis[child]){
                    vis[child] = 1;
                    q.push(child);
                }
            }
        }
        
        return ans;
    }
};

01/08/23, 14:30 - Gunjan Sharma: void dfs(int node,vector<bool> &vis,vector<int> &ans,vector<int> adj[]){
        ans.push_back(node);
        vis[node]=true;
        for(auto x:adj[node]){
            if(!vis[x])dfs(x,vis,ans,adj);
        }
    }
    vector<int> dfsOfGraph(int V, vector<int> adj[]) {
        // Code here
        vector<int> ans;
        vector<bool> vis(V,false);
        for(int i=0;i<V;i++){
            if(!vis[i])dfs(i,vis,ans,adj);
        }
        return ans;
    }
02/08/23, 18:47 - Gunjan Sharma: class Solution {
  public:
    int shortestDistance(int N, int M, vector<vector<int>> A, int X, int Y) {
        // code here
        queue<pair<int,pair<int,int>>> q;
        q.push({0,{0,0}});
        int dx[] = {-1,1,0,0};
        int dy[] = {0,0,1,-1};
        while(q.size()!=0){
            auto temp = q.front();
            q.pop();
            int dis=temp.first;
            int i=temp.second.first;
            int j=temp.second.second;
            if(i==X and j==Y)return dis;
            for(int k=0;k<4;k++){
                int newi = i+dx[k];
                int newj = j+dy[k];
                if(newi>=0 and newj>=0 and newi<N and newj<M and A[newi][newj]==1){
                    A[newi][newj]=0;
                    q.push({dis+1,{newi,newj}});
                }
            }
        }
        return -1;
    }
};

03/08/23, 12:37 - Gunjan Sharma: lass Solution {
  private:
    void topoSort(int node, vector < pair < int, int >> adj[],
      int vis[], stack < int > & st) {
      //This is the function to implement Topological sort. 
      vis[node] = 1;
      for (auto it: adj[node]) {
        int v = it.first;
        if (!vis[v]) {
          topoSort(v, adj, vis, st);
        }
      }
      st.push(node);
    }
  public:
    vector < int > shortestPath(int N, int M, vector < vector < int >> & edges) {

      //We create a graph first in the form of an adjacency list.
      vector < pair < int, int >> adj[N];
      for (int i = 0; i < M; i++) {
        int u = edges[i][0];
        int v = edges[i][1];
        int wt = edges[i][2];
        adj[u].push_back({v, wt}); 
      }
      // A visited array is created with initially 
      // all the nodes marked as unvisited (0).
      int vis[N] = {
        0
      };
      //Now, we perform topo sort using DFS technique 
      //and store the result in the stack st.
      stack < int > st;
      for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        if (!vis[i]) {
          topoSort(i, adj, vis, st);
        }
      }
      //Further, we declare a vector â€˜distâ€™ in which we update the value of the nodesâ€™
      //distance from the source vertex after relaxation of a particular node.

      vector < int > dist(N);
      for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        dist[i] = 1e9;
      }

      dist[0] = 0;
      while (!st.empty()) {
        int node = st.top();
        st.pop();

        for (auto it: adj[node]) {
          int v = it.first;
          int wt = it.second;

          if (dist[node] + wt < dist[v]) {
            dist[v] = wt + dist[node];
          }
        }
      }

      for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        if (dist[i] == 1e9) dist[i] = -1;
      }
      return dist;
    }
};

04/08/23, 13:42 - Gunjan Sharma: class Solution{
public:
    void Reverse(stack<int> &St){
        if(St.empty()){
            return;
        }
        int x=St.top();
        St.pop();
        Reverse(St);
        
        insert(St,x);
    }
    
    void insert(stack<int> &St, int value){
        if(St.empty()){
            St.push(value);
            return;
        }
        int x=St.top();
        St.pop();
        insert(St,value);
        
        St.push(x);
    }
};

05/08/23, 11:48 - Gunjan Sharma: class Solution{ 
public:
    long long findMinDiff(vector<long long> a, long long n, long long m){
    //code
    sort(a.begin(), a.end());
    long long i=0,j=m-1;
    
    long long ans = INT_MAX;
    while(j<n){
        ans  = min(ans,a[j]-a[i]);
        i++;
        j++;
    }
    return ans;
    
    }   
};

06/08/23, 14:16 - Gunjan Sharma: class Solution{
    public:
    void help(string str,vector<string>& ans, int freq[], string S ){
        if(str.size()== S.size()){
            ans.push_back(str);
            return;
        }
        
        for(int i=0;i<S.size();i++){
            if(!freq[i]){
                str.push_back(S[i]);
                freq[i]=1;
                help(str,ans,freq,S);
                freq[i]=0;
                str.pop_back();
            }
        }
    }
    
    vector<string> permutation(string S)
    {
        int n=S.size();
        vector<string> ans;
        int freq[n];
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++) freq[i]=0;
        help("",ans,freq,S);
        sort(ans.begin(),ans.end());
        return ans;
    }
};

07/08/23, 19:55 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution 
{
    public:
    //Function to find a solved Sudoku. 
    bool SolveSudoku(int grid[N][N])  
    { 
        solve(grid);
    }
    bool solve(int grid[N][N]){
        for(int i=0;i<N;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<N;j++){
                if(grid[i][j]==0){
                    
                    for(int d=1;d<=9;d++){
                        if(isValid(grid, i, j, d)){
                            grid[i][j]=d;
                            
                            if(solve(grid)==true){
                                return true;
                            }
                            else{
                                grid[i][j]=0;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        return true;
    }
    
    bool isValid(int grid[N][N], int row, int col, int d){
        for(int i=0;i<9;i++){
            if(grid[row][i]==d) return false;
            if(grid[i][col]==d) return false;
            
            if(grid[ 3*(row/3)+ i/3 ][ 3*(col/3) +i%3 ]==d ) return false;
        }
        
        return true;
    }
    
    //Function to print grids of the Sudoku.
    void printGrid (int grid[N][N]) 
    {
        if(SolveSudoku(grid)){
            for(int i=0;i<N;i++){
                for(int j=0;j<N;j++){
                    cout<<grid[i][j]<<" ";
                }
            }
        }
    }
};

09/08/23, 21:09 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution{
public: 
    bool prime(int n) {
        if (n == 2) return true;

        for (int i = 2; i <= sqrt(n); i++) {
            if (n % i == 0) return false;
        }

        return true;
    }
    long long int largestPrimeFactor(int N){
        if (prime(N)) return N;

        long ans = -1;

        for (int i = 2; i <= sqrt(N); i++) {
            if (N % i == 0) {
                if (prime(i)) ans = max(ans,long(i));
                if (prime(N / i)) ans = max(ans,long(N / i));
            }
        }

        return ans;
    }
};

10/08/23, 20:29 - Gunjan Sharma: public:
    int lcs(int n, int m , string str1, string str2) {
        int A = str1.length();
        int B = str2.length();
        
        vector<vector<int>> dp(A + 1, vector<int>(B + 1, 0));
        
        for (int i = 1; i <= A; ++i) {
            for (int j = 1; j <= B; ++j) {
                if (str1[i - 1] == str2[j - 1]) {
                    dp[i][j] = 1 + dp[i - 1][j - 1];
                } else {
                    dp[i][j] = max(dp[i - 1][j], dp[i][j - 1]);
                }
            }
        }
        
        return dp[A][B];
    }
};

11/08/23, 15:28 - Gunjan Sharma: public:
    long long int help(int ind, int N, int coins[], int sum,vector<vector<long long int>>& dp){
        if(ind==N-1){
            return (sum%coins[N-1]==0);
        }
        
        if(dp[ind][sum]!=-1){
            return dp[ind][sum];
        }
        
        long long int notTake= help(ind+1,N,coins,sum,dp);
        long long int take=0;
        if(coins[ind]<=sum){
            take=help(ind,N,coins,sum-coins[ind],dp);
        }
        
        return dp[ind][sum]= take+notTake;
    }
  
    long long int count(int coins[], int N, int sum) {
        vector<vector<long long int>> dp(N,vector< long long int>(sum+1,-1));
        return help(0,N,coins,sum,dp);
    }
};

12/08/23, 22:03 - Gunjan Sharma: class Solution
{
     public:
    int longestSubsequence(int n, int a[])
    {
       vector<int> ans;
       ans.push_back(a[0]);
       for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
           if(a[i]>ans.back()){
               ans.push_back(a[i]);
           }
           else{
               int ind= lower_bound(ans.begin(),ans.end(), a[i])- ans.begin();
               ans[ind]=a[i];
           }
       }
       return ans.size();
    }
};

  public:
  int mod=1e9+7;
  int nthFibonacci(int n){
          if(n==0) return 0;
          if(n==1) return 1;
          int a=0,b=1,c;
          for(int i=2;i<=n;i++){
              c=(a+b)%mod;
              a=b;
              b=c;
          }
          return c;
    }
};

14/08/23, 11:28 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
public:
    vector<int> singleNumber(vector<int> arr) 
    {
       int n = arr.size();
        int all = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
            all = all ^ arr[i];

        // Find the rightmost set bit
        int m = all & -all;

        // Separate the numbers into two groups
        int g1 = 0, g2 = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            if ((m & arr[i]) == 0) {
                g1 ^= arr[i];
            } else {
                g2 ^= arr[i];
            }
        }

        std::vector<int> ans;
        if (g1 > g2) {
            ans.push_back(g2);
            ans.push_back(g1);
        } else {
            ans.push_back(g1);
            ans.push_back(g2);
        }

        return ans;
    }
};

15/08/23, 09:20 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution{
    public:
    int maxOnes(int a[], int n)
    {
       int count =0;
       int one = 0;
       int max=0;
       
       for( int i =0; i<n; i++){
           if(a[i] ==0){
           count++;}
           else{
               count--;
               one++;
               if(count<0){
                   count=0;
               }
           }
           if(count>max){
               max= count;
           }
       }
       return max+one;
    }
};

16/08/23, 10:33 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
    public:
    //Function to find the nth catalan number.
    const int m = 1000000007;
    
    int findCatalan(int n) 
    {
        long long dp[n+1];
    dp[0] = 1; dp[1] = 1;
    for (int i = 2; i <= n; i++) {
        dp[i] = 0;
        for (int j = 0; j < i; j++) {
            dp[i] = (dp[i] + (dp[j] * dp[i - j - 1]) % m) % m;
        }
    }
    return (int)dp[n];
    }
}; <This message was edited>

17/08/23, 09:41 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution{
public:
	vector<int> generateNextPalindrome(int a[], int n) {
	    // code a
	    vector<int> ans;
	    int i,j, carry, solved=0;
	    for( i=(n)/2; i<n ;i++)
	    {
	        if(a[i] < a[n-i-1])
	        {
	            a[i] = a[n-i-1];
	            for(j=i+1; j<n ;j++)
	            {
	                a[j] = a[n-j-1];
	            }
	            
	            solved=1;
	            break;
	        }
	        else if(a[i] > a[n-i-1])
	        break;
	    }
	    if(solved==1)
	    {
    	    for(i=0; i<n; i++)
    	    {
    	        ans.push_back(a[i]);
    	    }
    	    
    	    return ans;
	    }
	    
	    // decremental case
	    else{
	    carry=1;
	    for(i=(n-1)/2; i>=0 ;i--)
	    {
	        if(a[i] + carry ==10)
	        {
	            a[i] =0; carry=1;
	        }
	        else
	        {
	            a[i]++; carry=0; break;
	        }
	    }
	    //
	    if(carry==1)
	    ans.push_back(1);
	    
	    for(i=0; i<n; i++)
	    ans.push_back(a[i]);
	    
	    if(carry==1) n++;
	    
	    for(i=(n+1)/2 ;i<n; i++)
	    ans[i] = ans[n-i-1];
	    
	    return ans;
	    }
	}
};

    //Function to find the leaders in the array.
    public:
    vector<int> leaders(int a[], int n){
       vector<int> ans;
       int mx=INT_MIN;
       for(int i=n-1;i>=0;i--){
           if(a[i]>=mx){
               mx=a[i];
               ans.push_back(mx);
           }
       }
       
       reverse(ans.begin(),ans.end());
       return ans;
        
    }
};

19/08/23, 17:36 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
    public:
    //Function to find a continuous sub-array which adds up to a given number.
    vector<int> subarraySum(vector<int>arr, int n, long long s)
    {
         vector<int> result;
    bool found = false;
    int st = 0, end = 0;
    int sum = 0;
    
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        sum += arr[i];
        
        if (sum >= s) {
            end = i;
            while (s < sum && st < end) {
                sum -= arr[st++];
            }
        }
        
        if (sum == s) {
            result.push_back(st + 1);
            result.push_back(end + 1);
            found = true;
            break;
        }
    }
    
    if (!found)
        result.push_back(-1);
    
    return result;
    }
};

20/08/23, 09:22 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution {
    int count(int arr[], int n, int x) {
        // code here
        int left_index = bsli(arr,0,n-1,x);
        int right_index = bsri(arr,0,n-1,x);
        
        return right_index - left_index;
    }
    
    int bsli(int arr[], int l, int r, int x){
        while(l<=r){
            int mid = (l+r)/2;
            if(arr[mid]>=x) r = mid-1;
            else l = mid+1;
        }
        return r;
    }
    int bsri(int arr[], int l, int r, int x){
        while(l<=r){
            int mid = (l+r)/2;
            if(arr[mid]<=x) l = mid+1;
            else r = mid-1;
        }
        return r;
    }
};

21/08/23, 08:35 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution {
public:
    int Count(vector<vector<int>>& matrix) {
        int ans = 0;
        
        vector<int> row = {-1, -1, 0, 1, 1, 1, 0, -1};
        vector<int> col = {0, 1, 1, 1, 0, -1, -1, -1};
        int n = matrix.size();
        int m = matrix[0].size();
        
        for (int i = 0; i < matrix.size(); i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < matrix[0].size(); j++) {
                int count = 0;
                if (matrix[i][j] == 1) {
                    for (int k = 0; k < 8; k++) {
                        int r = i + row[k];
                        int c = j + col[k];
                        
                        if (r >= 0 && r < n && c >= 0 && c < m && matrix[r][c] == 0) {
                            count++;
                        }
                    }
                    if (count > 0 && count % 2 == 0) {
                        ans++;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return ans;
    }

};

22/08/23, 07:57 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
    public:
    //Function to find minimum number of operations that are required 
    //to make the matrix beautiful.
    int findMinOpeartion(vector<vector<int> > matrix, int n)
    {
        // code here 
        int sum = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
                sum = sum + matrix[i][j];
            }
        }
    
        int rs = 0;
        int cs = 0;
    
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            int a = 0;
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
                a = a + matrix[i][j];
            }
            rs = max(rs, a);
    
            int b = 0;
            for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
                b = b + matrix[j][i];
            }
            cs = max(cs, b);
        }
    
        int maxVal = max(cs, rs);
    
        return maxVal * n - sum;
    
    } 
};

23/08/23, 00:18 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution {
public:
	
	    // Code here
	    bool find(int i , int j , int indx , int flag , vector<vector<char>>&grid  , string &word){
       if( i >= grid.size() || i < 0 || j >= grid[0].size() || j < 0 || word[indx] != grid[i][j])
       return false;
       
       if(word[indx] == grid[i][j] && indx == word.size() -1)
       return true;
     
        if(flag == 1)  return find( i + 1 , j , indx + 1 , 1 , grid , word);
        if(flag == 2)  return find( i - 1 , j , indx + 1 , 2 , grid , word);
        if(flag == 3)  return find( i + 1 , j + 1, indx + 1 , 3 , grid , word);
        if(flag == 4)  return find( i + 1 , j - 1 , indx + 1 , 4 , grid , word);
        if(flag == 5)  return find( i , j + 1, indx + 1 , 5 , grid , word);
        if(flag == 6)  return find( i  , j -1 , indx + 1 , 6 , grid , word);
        if(flag == 7)  return find( i - 1 , j -1  , indx + 1 , 7 , grid , word);
        if(flag == 8)  return find( i - 1 , j + 1, indx + 1 , 8 , grid , word);
   }
    vector<vector<int>>searchWord(vector<vector<char>>grid, string word){
       int R = grid.size();
       int C = grid[0].size();
       vector<vector<int>>ans;
       for( int i = 0 ; i < R ; i++)
       for( int j = 0 ; j < C ; j++)
       for (int flag = 1; flag <= 8; flag++) 
                if (find(i, j, 0, flag, grid, word)) {
                    ans.push_back({i, j});
                    break;  // No need to check other directions for this cell
                }
            
       
       return ans;
    }
    
	
};

24/08/23, 16:45 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
    public String multiplyStrings(String s1,String s2)
    {
        //code here.
        int n1=s1.length();
        int n2 = s2.length();
        int a = s1.charAt(0)=='-'?-1:0;
        int b = s2.charAt(0)=='-'?-1:0;
        
        int arr[] =  new int[n1+n2];
        for(int i=n1-1; i>=0; i--){
            int k = i+n2;
            if(s1.charAt(i)!='-'){
                int carry = 0;
                for(int j=n2-1; j>=0; j--){
                    if(s2.charAt(j)!='-'){
                        
                        int x = (s1.charAt(i)-'0')*(s2.charAt(j)-'0') + carry + arr[k];
                        arr[k] = x %10;
                        carry = x/10;
                        k--;
                    }
                }
                if(carry>0){
                    arr[k] = carry;
                }
            }
        }
        boolean flag = true;
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        for(int i=0; i<n1+n2; i++){
            while(i<n1+n2 && flag==true && arr[i]==0){
                i++;
            }
            flag =false;
            if(i<n1+n2) sb.append(arr[i]);
        }
        String str = sb.toString();
        if(a<0 && b>=0 || a>=0 && b<0) str = "-"+str;
        if(str.length()==0) return "0";
        return str;
    }
}

26/08/23, 09:39 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution{
  public:
    int longestKSubstr(string s, int k) {
        int i = 0, j = 0, n = s.length(), maxi = INT_MIN;
        set<char>st;
        map<char, int>mp;
        while(j < n){
            st.insert(s[j]);
            mp[s[j]]++;
            if(st.size() == k) maxi = max(maxi, j-i+1);
            if(st.size() > k) {
                mp[s[i]]--;
                if(mp[s[i]] == 0) st.erase(s[i]);
                i++;
            }
            j++;
        }
        if(maxi == INT_MIN) return -1;
        return maxi;
    }
};

27/08/23, 22:12 - Garima: Solution
{
    public:
    string reverseWord(string str)
    {
        for(int i = 0; i < str.size() / 2; i++){
            swap(str[i], str[str.size() - i - 1]);
        }
        
        return str;
    }
};

28/08/23, 11:58 - Gunjan Sharma: Node *removeDuplicates(Node *head)
{
 // your code goes here
 if(head==NULL){
     return head;
 }
 
 Node* temp = head->next;
 Node* prev = head;
 
 while(temp!=NULL){
     if(temp->data==prev->data){
         prev->next = temp->next;
         temp = prev->next;
     }else{
         prev = temp;
         temp = temp->next;
     }
 }
 return head;
}

29/08/23, 09:30 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
    public:
    Node *compute(Node *head)
    {
        // your code goes here
        if(!head or !head->next) return head;
        stack<int> st;
        while(head)
        {
            while(!st.empty() and st.top()<head->data) st.pop();
            st.push(head->data);
            head=head->next;
        }
        
        Node* temp = NULL;
        while(!st.empty())
        {
            Node* tempo = new Node(st.top());
            st.pop();
            tempo->next=temp;
            temp=tempo;
        }
        return temp;
    }
    
};

{
    //Your code here
    if(x == 1)
        return head->next;
    Node* ptr = head;
    x = x-2;
    while(x--)
        ptr = ptr->next;    
    Node* curr = ptr->next;
    ptr->next = ptr->next->next;

}

31/08/23, 13:55 - Gunjan Sharma: void getElements(Node* root, vector<int>& inorder, int data){
    if(!root)
        return;
    getElements(root -> left, inorder, data);
    if(data != root -> data)
        inorder.push_back(root -> data);
    getElements(root -> right, inorder, data);
}

Node* getBalancedTree(vector<int> elements, int height){
    if(elements.size() == 0){
        return NULL;
    }
    int mid = elements.size() >> 1;
    Node* temp = new Node(elements[mid]);
    temp -> height = height;
    if(elements.size() == 1){
        
        return temp;
    }
    vector<int> left(elements.begin(), elements.begin() + mid), right(elements.begin() + mid + 1, elements.end());
    temp -> left = getBalancedTree(left, height + 1);
    temp -> right = getBalancedTree(right, height + 1);
    return temp;
    
}

Node* deleteNode(Node* root, int data)
{
    vector<int> inorder;
    getElements(root, inorder, data);
    return getBalancedTree(inorder, 1);
}

02/09/23, 10:19 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
public:
    int getCount(Node *root, int k)
    {
        queue<Node*> q;
        q.push(root);
        int cnt=0,level=1;
        while(!q.empty())
        {
            int size=q.size();
            while(size--)
            {
                Node* temp=q.front();
                q.pop();
                if(temp->left==NULL and temp->right==NULL and k>=level)
                {
                    k-=level;
                    cnt++;
                }
                if(temp->left) q.push(temp->left);
                if(temp->right) q.push(temp->right);
            }
            level++;
        }
        return cnt;
    }
};

03/09/23, 18:29 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution {
public:
    bool isIsomorphic(Node *root1, Node *root2) {
        // base condition
        if (!root1 && !root2)
            return true;
        
        if ((!root1 && root2) || (root1 && !root2))
            return false;
        
        if (root1->data != root2->data)
            return false;
        
        return (isIsomorphic(root1->left, root2->left) && isIsomorphic(root1->right, root2->right))
            || (isIsomorphic(root1->left, root2->right) && isIsomorphic(root1->right, root2->left));
    }
};

05/09/23, 11:35 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution {
  public:
    // Function to return the adjacency list for each vertex.
     vector<vector<int>> printGraph(int V, vector<pair<int,int>>edges) {
        // Code here
        vector<vector<int>> list(V);
        for(auto it : edges){
            list[it.first].push_back(it.second);
            list[it.second].push_back(it.first);
        }
        return list;
    }
};

06/09/23, 21:50 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution 
{
    public:
    //Function to find a Mother Vertex in the Graph.
	int findMotherVertex(int V, vector<int>adj[])
	{
	    vector<int> order;
	    vector<bool> vis(V, 0);
	    
	    function<void(int)> dfs1 = [&](int node) {
	        vis[node] = 1;
	        
	        for(auto child : adj[node])
	            if(!vis[child])
	                dfs1(child);
	                
	        order.push_back(node);
	    };
	    
	    for(int i = 0; i < V; i++){
	        if(!vis[i])
	            dfs1(i);
	    }
	    
	    fill(vis.begin(), vis.end(), 0);
	    
	    int rem = V;
	    
	    function<void(int)> dfs2 = [&](int node) {
	        vis[node] = 1;
	        --rem;
	        
	        for(auto child : adj[node])
	            if(!vis[child])
	                dfs2(child);
	    };
	    
	    dfs2(order.back());
	    
	    return (rem == 0) ? order.back() : -1;
	}

};

08/09/23, 18:43 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution{
  public:
    // The given root is the root of the Binary Tree
    // Return the root of the generated BST
    void inorder(Node* root, vector<int> &ans){
         if(root==NULL) return;
        inorder(root->left, ans);
       
        ans.push_back(root->data);
        inorder(root->right,ans);
    }
    int i=0;
    void dfs(Node* root, vector<int>& ans){
         if(root==NULL) return;
        dfs(root->left, ans);
      
        root->data=ans[i];
        i++;
        dfs(root->right,ans);
    }
    Node *binaryTreeToBST (Node *root)
    {
        //Your code goes here
        vector<int> ans;
        inorder(root,ans);
        sort(ans.begin(),ans.end());
        dfs(root,ans);
        return root;
    }
};

09/09/23, 16:29 - Gunjan Sharma: if (input1 < 4) {
            throw std::invalid_argument("EmptyReturnValue");
        }

        int minCost[input1];

        // Base cases
        minCost[0] = input2[0];
        minCost[1] = input2[1];
        minCost[2] = input2[2];

        // Fill the array using dynamic programming
        for (int i = 3; i < input1; i++) {
            minCost[i] = std::min(minCost[i - 1], minCost[i - 3]) + input2[i];
        }

        // Return the minimum cost to reach the last city
        return minCost[input1 - 1];
    }

09/09/23, 21:17 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
    public:
    
       void reverse_inorder( Node * root , vector<int> &ans){
           
           if(root == NULL){
               return;
           }
           
           reverse_inorder(root->right , ans);
           ans.push_back(root->data);
           reverse_inorder(root->left , ans);
       }
    int kthLargest(Node *root, int K)
    {
       vector<int> ans;                       // it is very simple question and we can solve this question
                                             // in two way 1.reverse_inorder traversal and store the data in Descending Order
       reverse_inorder(root , ans);          // where the k largest element is present on k - 1 index of vector 
                                              // 2. By useing Max Priority Queue and store the root data in Max heap
                                              // After store data pop(); k-1  element for Max heap and return top of Priority Queue 
       if( K > ans.size()){                   // Notice -: Might the time - complexity will increase in second approach.
           return -1;
       }
       
       return ans[K-1];
    }
};
10/09/23, 15:08 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
    public:
        Node* insert(Node* node, int data) {
        
            // firstly we put data in newnode
            Node *newNode = new Node(data);
            
            // there is  3 conditons
            
            // First node or root is empty 
            // this means this is first node we return this node
            if(node==NULL) return newNode;
            
            //second condition
            // root exist or node exist
            // if the inserting node data is bigger than root data
            
            if(data>node->data)
            {
                //now we check its right exist 
                // if yes we go again right 
                // else we insert newnode
                
                if(node->right!=NULL)insert(node->right,data);
                else node->right = newNode; 
            }
            
            
            //third contion 
            // root exist or node exist
            // if the inserting node data is smaller than root data
            else if(data<node->data)
            {
                // now we check its left exist 
                // if yes then we go again left
                // else we insert newnode
                
                if(node->left!=NULL)
                {
                    insert(node->left,data);
                   
                }
                else node->left = newNode;
            }
            
            return node;
    }

};

12/09/23, 22:33 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution {
  public:
    int isPerfectNumber(long long N) {
        // code here
        if(N==1)    return 0;
        long long count=1;
        long long factor1,factor2;
        for(long long i=2;i<=sqrt(N);i++){
            if(N%i==0){
                factor1=i;
                factor2=N/i;
                count=count+factor1+factor2;
            }
        }
        if(count==N)    return 1;
        return 0;
    }
};

13/09/23, 16:47 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution{
public:
    string findLargest(int N, int S){
        // code here
        // The result string
        string res = "";
    
        // Special case handling for S = 0
        if (S == 0) {
            if (N == 1) {
                return "0";
            } else {
                return "-1";
            }
        }
    
        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
            // For every slot, find the largest possible digit
            for (int d = 9; d >= 0; d--) {
                if (d <= S) {
                    // Place the digit in the result
                    res += to_string(d);
                    
                    // Reduce the sum
                    S -= d;
                    
                    break;  // break the inner loop and move to next slot
                }
            }
        }
    
        // If there's still some sum left, it means it's not possible to form the number
        if (S > 0) {
            return "-1";
        }
        
        return res;
    }
};

14/09/23, 19:10 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution{

	public:
	int perfectSum(int arr[], int n, int sum)
{
    const int MOD = 1e9 + 7;
       
 vector<vector<int>> dp(n + 1, vector<int>(sum + 1, 0));
 
    // Initialize the dp array
    dp[0][0] = 1;
    for (int j = 1; j <= sum; j++)
        dp[0][j] = 0;
 
    // Fill the dp array
    for (int i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j <= sum; j++) {
            if (arr[i - 1] <= j)
                dp[i][j] = (dp[i - 1][j] + dp[i - 1][j - arr[i - 1]]) % MOD;
            else
                dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j];
        }
    }
 
    return dp[n][sum];
        
}
	  
};

15/09/23, 19:13 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution{
public:
    int equalPartition(int N, int arr[])
    {
        function<int()> checkOdd = [&]()->int{
            int flag = 0;
            for(int i =0; i< N; i++) flag ^=arr[i];
            return flag & 1;
        };
        if(checkOdd()) return 0;
        
        
        int target = 0;
        for(int i =0; i< N; i++) target += arr[i];
        target /=2;
        vector<int> subsets(target+1, 0);
        subsets[0]=1;
        for (int i =0; i<N; i++){
            if(arr[i] > target) return 0;
            for(int j = target; j >= arr[i]; j--){
                subsets[j] += subsets[j-arr[i]];
            }
        }
        return (subsets[target] != 0);
    }
};

19/09/23, 19:17 - Gunjan Sharma: Solution
{
    public:
    //Function to find position of first set bit in the given number.
    unsigned int getFirstSetBit(int n)
    {
        unsigned int x = 1;
        if(n == 0) return 0;
        while(n > 0)
        {
            
            if(n%2 == 0) x++;
            else
            {
                break;
            }
            n = n/2;
        }
        
        return x;
    }


};
